data-gt="&#123;&quot;action_type&quot;:&quot;1&quot;,&quot;aggregation_id&quot;:&quot;10151674319973229&quot;,&quot;aggregation_time&quot;:&quot;1377008183&quot;,&quot;actor&quot;:&quot;85604478228&quot;,&quot;creator&quot;:&quot;85604478228&quot;,&quot;pagestimeline&quot;:&quot;1&quot;,&quot;payload_type&quot;:&quot;7&quot;,&quot;eventtime&quot;:&quot;1377634314&quot;,&quot;viewerid&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;profileownerid&quot;:&quot;85604478228&quot;,&quot;unitimpressionid&quot;:&quot;a7d03737&quot;,&quot;contentid&quot;:&quot;4864325823670812508&quot;,&quot;timeline_unit_type&quot;:&quot;AddSinglePhotoUnit&quot;,&quot;timewindowsize&quot;:&quot;3&quot;,&quot;query_type&quot;:&quot;36&quot;,&quot;contextwindowstart&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;contextwindowend&quot;:&quot;1378018799&quot;&#125;" data-time="1377008183"><div class=""><div role="article"><div class="clearfix mbs pbs _1_m"><a class="_51wa _29h _303" href="https://www.facebook.com/pages/BIG-ARTS-Music-Arts-and-Entertainment/85604478228?hc_location=timeline" data-ft="&#123;&quot;tn&quot;:&quot;\\u003C&quot;&#125;" tabindex="-1" data-ft="&#123;&quot;tn&quot;:&quot;C&quot;&#125;"><span class="fcg"><span class="fwb" data-ft="&#123;&quot;tn&quot;:&quot;;&quot;&#125;"><a href="https://www.facebook.com/pages/BIG-ARTS-Music-Arts-and-Entertainment/85604478228?hc_location=timeline">BIG ARTS - Music, Arts, and Entertainment</a></span></span> </h5><div class="_1_n fsm fwn fcg"><a class="uiLinkSubtle" href="https://www.facebook.com/photo.php?fbid=10151674319973229&amp;set=a.135797518228.110834.85604478228&amp;type=1"><abbr title="Tuesday, August 20, 2013 at 7:16am" data-utime="1377008183">August 20</abbr></a><a data-hover="tooltip" aria-label="Public" class="uiStreamPrivacy inlineBlock fbStreamPrivacy fbPrivacyAudienceIndicator _1_o" href="#" role="button"><i class="lock img sp_8u5rsk sx_f7667f"></i></a></div></div></div><div class="aboveUnitContent"><div class="userContentWrapper"><div class="_wk"><span class="userContent"><div id="id_521d080b1706a4788982793" class="text_exposed_root">Auditions on August 27 and 28 for BIG ARTS Community Players:<br /> <br /> Open auditions for the comedy-mystery, &quot;Art of Murder&quot; will be held 7 to 9 p.m. on Tuesday, August 27 and Wednesday, August 28 at Herb Strauss Theater, 2200 Periwinkle Way, Sani<span class="text_exposed_hide">...</span><span class="text_exposed_show">bel. <br /> All actors must bring a headshot and resume to the casting call. Produced by the Community Players, &quot;Art of Murder&quot; will  feature volunteers onstage and backstage.<br /> <br /> Director Peter Stearns is seeking two female and two male actors. The characters are: <br /> 1.	Jack (age late 30s to early 50s) - an eccentric and ruggedly handsome artist.<br /> 2.	Vincent (age 30s to 60s) - a high-powered flamboyant art dealer.<br /> 3.	Annie (age late 20 to 30s) - Jack’s beautiful wife who is an artist.<br /> 4.	Kate (age 20 to 30) - an immigrant maid from Ireland.<br /> <br /> &quot;Art of Murder&quot; will be performed at the Herb Strauss Theater on Thursdays, Fridays and Saturdays, from October 24 to November 9. All shows will be at 8 p.m.<br /> <br /> The 2000 Edgar Award Winner for Best Mystery Play, &quot;Art of Murder&quot; was written by Joe DiPietro. This dark comedy is set in a remote estate in the countryside of Connecticut as Jack awaits the arrival of Vincent. However, the visit is unusual because Jack believes he has been wronged and he is intending to kill Vincent. As Jack plans his evening, Annie calmly paints. She is reluctant to go along with the plan until Jack&#039;s threat of violence convinces her otherwise. Harried and annoyed, Vincent arrives. Will Jack carry out his plan? Will Annie help him? Or, is something else going on? <br /> <br /> Rehearsals will begin Wednesday, September 18 and will continue on Monday, September 23, Wednesday September 25, and Thursday September 26. All rehearsals are from 7 to 9 p.m. and additional rehearsals will be scheduled as needed.  <br /> <br /> All performances are at 8 p.m. and are scheduled for Thursday, October 24, Friday, October 25, Saturday, October 6, Thursday, October 31, Friday, November 1, Saturday, November 2, Thursday, November 7, Friday, November 8 and Saturday, November 9 at Herb Strauss Theater.<br /> <br /> The Community Players are also in need of volunteers to help with set-building, prop acquisition, stage managing and stage hands for theater productions. Audition and cast information is available on <a href="http://www.facebook.com/l.php?u=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.bigarts.org%2Fmedia.php&amp;h=TAQH0lGiZ&amp;s=1" rel="nofollow nofollow" target="_blank" onmouseover="LinkshimAsyncLink.swap(this, &quot;http:\\/\\/www.bigarts.org\\/media.php&quot;);" onclick="LinkshimAsyncLink.swap(this, &quot;http:\\/\\/www.facebook.com\\/l.php?u=http\\u00253A\\u00252F\\u00252Fwww.bigarts.org\\u00252Fmedia.php&amp;h=TAQH0lGiZ&amp;s=1&quot;);">http://www.bigarts.org/media.php</a><br /> <br /> The Community Players provide local live theater, performed for the community, by the community.</span><span class="text_exposed_hide"><span class="text_exposed_link"><a onclick="var parent = Parent.byClass(this, &quot;text_exposed_root&quot;); if (parent &amp;&amp; parent.getAttribute(&quot;id&quot;) == &quot;id_521d080b1706a4788982793&quot;) &#123; CSS.addClass(parent, &quot;text_exposed&quot;); Arbiter.inform(&quot;reflow&quot;); &#125;" data-ft="&#123;&quot;tn&quot;:&quot;e&quot;&#125;">See More</a></span></span></div></span></div></div></div><div class="photoUnit clearfix"><div class="_53s uiScaledThumb photo photoWidth1" data-gt="&#123;&quot;fbid&quot;:&quot;10151674319973229&quot;&#125;" data-ft="&#123;&quot;tn&quot;:&quot;E&quot;&#125;"><a class="_6i9" href="https://www.facebook.com/photo.php?fbid=10151674319973229&amp;set=a.135797518228.110834.85604478228&amp;type=1&amp;relevant_count=1" rel="theater" ajaxify="https://www.facebook.com/photo.php?fbid=10151674319973229&amp;set=a.135797518228.110834.85604478228&amp;type=1&amp;relevant_count=1&amp;src=https%3A%2F%2Ffbcdn-sphotos-b-a.akamaihd.net%2Fhphotos-ak-prn2%2F1185180_10151674319973229_483974341_n.jpg&amp;size=450%2C242&amp;theater&amp;source=9"><div class="uiScaledImageContainer photoWrap" style="height:242px;"><img class="img" src="https://fbcdn-sphotos-b-a.akamaihd.net/hphotos-ak-prn2/p480x480/1185180_10151674319973229_483974341_n.jpg" alt="Photo: Auditions on August 27 and 28 for BIG ARTS Community Players:

Open auditions for the comedy-mystery, &quot;Art of Murder&quot; will be held 7 to 9 p.m. on Tuesday, August 27 and Wednesday, August 28 at Herb Strauss Theater, 2200 Periwinkle Way, Sanibel. 
All actors must bring a headshot and resume to the casting call. Produced by the Community Players, &quot;Art of Murder&quot; will  feature volunteers onstage and backstage.

Director Peter Stearns is seeking two female and two male actors. The characters are: 
1.	Jack (age late 30s to early 50s) - an eccentric and ruggedly handsome artist.
2.	Vincent (age 30s to 60s) - a high-powered flamboyant art dealer.
3.	Annie (age late 20 to 30s) - Jack&#x2019;s beautiful wife who is an artist.
4.	Kate (age 20 to 30) - an immigrant maid from Ireland.

&quot;Art of Murder&quot; will be performed at the Herb Strauss Theater on Thursdays, Fridays and Saturdays, from October 24 to November 9. All shows will be at 8 p.m.

The 2000 Edgar Award Winner for Best Mystery Play, &quot;Art of Murder&quot; was written by Joe DiPietro. This dark comedy is set in a remote estate in the countryside of Connecticut as Jack awaits the arrival of Vincent. However, the visit is unusual because Jack believes he has been wronged and he is intending to kill Vincent. As Jack plans his evening, Annie calmly paints. She is reluctant to go along with the plan until Jack&#039;s threat of violence convinces her otherwise. Harried and annoyed, Vincent arrives. Will Jack carry out his plan? Will Annie help him? Or, is something else going on? 

Rehearsals will begin Wednesday, September 18 and will continue on Monday, September 23, Wednesday September 25, and Thursday September 26. All rehearsals are from 7 to 9 p.m. and additional rehearsals will be scheduled as needed.  

All performances are at 8 p.m. and are scheduled for Thursday, October 24, Friday, October 25, Saturday, October 6, Thursday, October 31, Friday, November 1, Saturday, November 2, Thursday, November 7, Friday, November 8 and Saturday, November 9 at Herb Strauss Theater.

The Community Players are also in need of volunteers to help with set-building, prop acquisition, stage managing and stage hands for theater productions. Audition and cast information is available on http://www.bigarts.org/media.php

The Community Players provide local live theater, performed for the community, by the community." width="450" height="242" /></div></a></div></div></div><div class="fbTimelineUFI photos)</span></div><div class="userContentWrapper"><div><span class="userContent"><div id="id_521d080b1b6434949124838" class="text_exposed_root">A Community Theater fun-filled original musical playing at the Herb Strauss Theater through July 20th.  <br />  <br /> “Jersey Girls” cast includes Anna Anderson, Noelle Aparte, Russell Bias, Sabrina Chantel, Gia Corbeil, Sarah Daigle, Linda Fazioli, A<span class="text_exposed_hide">...</span><span class="text_exposed_show">nna Grilli, Scott Knop, Lisa Kuchinski, Shelley Sanders and Tyler Young. This production features choreography by Bobbi Frasca, props and costume design by Ana Perez, musical direction by Nancy Fueyo and historical research by Jack Koc, with lighting and sound design by BIG ARTS Technical Director Adam Trummel. <br /> Co-writer and director, June Koc, “Jersey Girls,” came about because her husband, Jack, adores the 60s era of music. Koc and Nancy Fueyo channeled their mutual love for Seaside Heights into this musical about the popular Jersey Shore boardwalk.</span><span class="text_exposed_hide"><span class="text_exposed_link"><a
